Sepiaうまそ思い出してうえってなってるFun fact: The color, "sepia", is named after the pigment, "sepia", which is extracted from a species of cuttlefish, whose greek name transliterates to "sepia". Thus, "sepia tone" means, literally, "the color of the pigment of the cuttlefish."フリスクたこ焼きほんとにまずかったあったな懐かしw わー、確かにそれはバイタリティ溢れてるねぇ Baik, Kak Sepia. Sama-sama.
